***chaser.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a> (52214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">chacer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">chasour</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chaceür</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chaceor</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chacier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to chase, hunt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> senses from or influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chase</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pursue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chasseur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chasers.html>chasers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person or thing (ship, plane, car, etc.) that chases. <span class="defdate">[from 14th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  David Oatman,  <cite>Old Favorites, New Fun</cite>, page 32:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">One student <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b> and the other <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the chasee. Give the chasee three <a href = vnd.unilang:seconds.html>seconds</a> to get away and then allow the <a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a> to attempt to tag the chasee.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hunter. <span class="defdate">[from 15th c.]</span></li>
<li>A person who does the chasing on metalwork.</li>
<li>A horse: <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">originally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a horse used for hunting; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a horse trained for steeplechasing, a steeplechaser. <span class="defdate">[from 14th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>2002</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>Nick</a> Mordin, <i>Betting for a Living</i>, page 351:
<dl><dd>"[I]<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> looked like The Fellow <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> steeplechaser in many years. He'd earned the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> speed rating I'd ever given a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b>."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2003</b>, Avalyn Hunter, <i>American Classic Pedigrees 1914-2002</i>, page 458:
<dl><dd>"Wild Risk...<a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> his greatest successes as a steeplechaser rather than a <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> racer... <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chase</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">groove; decorate metal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chasers.html>chasers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Someone who chases <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">decorates</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> metal; a person who decorates metal by engraving or embossing. <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1863</b>, Virginia <a href = vnd.unilang:penny.html>Penny</a>, <i>The Employments of Women: A Cyclopaedia of Woman's Work</i>, page 100:
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a> B., heraldic <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b>, says there are several processes in making heraldy plates, sketching, engraving, embossing, chasing and burnishing."</dd>
<dd>"H. amp; C., manufacturers of cloth and <a href = vnd.unilang:gilt.html>gilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buttons.html>buttons</a>, say it requires some weeks to learn to chase the <a href = vnd.unilang:gilt.html>gilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buttons.html>buttons</a>, which are done with small metal tools and a hammer. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chasers.html>Chasers</a></b> are paid by the peice, working ten <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> a day, and some can earn $1 a day."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1971</b>, George <a href = vnd.unilang:bernard.html>Bernard</a> Hughes, <i>Living Crafts</i>, page 36:
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>Flat</a> chasing in sunken or low relief <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a technique by which the ornament <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed by beating down the ground from the front. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> done in essentially the same manner as repoussé work, where the ornament appears in high relief, but the design <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> punched from the face of the silver plate. ... Sometimes, instead of applying a freehand design, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a> the greased suface with a paper pattern in which the design <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> pricked with <a href = vnd.unilang:pins.html>pins</a>."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1972</b>, Richard <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>Came</a>, <i>Silver</i>, page 7:
<dl><dd>"Chasing in general can be distinguised from engraving, in that the design can be seen on the reverse or inside of the pieces. Having outlined the pattern on the surface, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:cuts.html>cuts</a> and at the same time slightly depresses the surface. A light hammer can be used in this process also."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A tool used for cleaning out screw threads, either as an integral part of a tap or <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> to remove waste material produced by the cutting tool, or as a separate tool to repair damaged threads. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1894</b>, <i>Machinery</i> (author(s) unknown), page 141:
<dl><dd>"In Fig. i <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> shown one of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chasers.html>chasers</a></b> in the position which it occupies in cutting a thread."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1918</b>, Franklin Day Jones, <i>Thread-cutting Methods: A Treatise on the Operation and Use of Various Tools and <a href = vnd.unilang:machines.html>Machines</a> for forming screw threads...</i>, page 32:
<dl><dd>"Many screw threads are also finished completely with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chasers.html>chasers</a></b> of this type, although they are not adapted for extremely acurate work unless the teeth are ground after hardening, because the pitch of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b> teeth <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> affected more or less by..."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1994</b>, Francis <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Farago, Mark A. <a href = vnd.unilang:curtis.html>Curtis</a>, <i>Handbook of Dimensional Measurement</i>, page 467:
<dl><dd>"The category of thread cutting tools inlcudes both the single-point and multiple-point [<b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b> type] lathe <a href = vnd.unilang:cutters.html>cutters</a>."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A chase gun.
<dl><dd><i>bow <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b>; stern <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></b></i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chateaubriand.html>chateaubriand</a> (94648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:chateaubriand.html>chateaubriand</a></i>, named after French Romantic writer <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois-Ren%C3%A9_de_Chateaubriand" class="extiw" title="w:François-René de Chateaubriand"><span class="Latn" lang="en">François-René <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chateaubriand.html>Chateaubriand</a></span></a>, who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to have enjoyed this type of <a href = vnd.unilang:steak.html>steak</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A thick, juicy cut from the center of a beef tenderloin.</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who <a href = vnd.unilang:chats.html>chats</a> or talks to excess.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> November 14,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blake_Bailey" class="extiw" title="w:Blake Bailey"><a href = vnd.unilang:blake.html>Blake</a> Bailey</a>,  “'Tennessee Williams,' by John Lahr  | print version: Theatrical victory of art <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> life, <i>International New York Times</i>, 18 November 2014, p. 13 | ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The New York Times">The New York Times</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/11/16/books/review/tennessee-williams-by-john-lahr.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[S]he [Edwina, mother of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tennessee_Williams" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tennessee Williams">Tennessee Williams</a>] <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> indeed <a href = vnd.unilang:amanda.html>Amanda</a> [Wingfield, character in Williams' play <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Glass_Menagerie" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Glass Menagerie">The Glass <a href = vnd.unilang:menagerie.html>Menagerie</a></a></i>] in the flesh: a doughty <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chatterbox.html>chatterbox</a></b> from Ohio who adopted the manner of a Southern <a href = vnd.unilang:belle.html>belle</a> and eschewed both <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> and sex to the greatest extent possible.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A cootie catcher <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">children's fortune-telling device</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Synonym of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chatterbot</i></span></span></li></ol>

***cheeseburger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburger.html>cheeseburger</a> (11889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Blend of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cheese</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a></i> (1928) 
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Cheeseburger.jpg/220px-Cheeseburger.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Cheeseburger.jpg/330px-Cheeseburger.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Cheeseburger.jpg/440px-Cheeseburger.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1800" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburger.html>cheeseburger</a>.</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburger.html>cheeseburger</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburgers.html>cheeseburgers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a> containing cheese (usually one or more <a href = vnd.unilang:slices.html>slices</a> of processed cheese).
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1956</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frank_O%27Hara" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Frank O | Hara"><a href = vnd.unilang:frank.html>Frank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:hara.html>Hara</a></a>,  <cite>A Step Away from Them</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.poetryfoundation.org/poems/42662/a-step-away-from-them">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Neon in daylight <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a / great pleasure, as Edwin Denby would / write, as are light bulbs in daylight. / I <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> for a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburger.html>cheeseburger</a></b> at <a href = vnd.unilang:juliet.html>Juliet</a>'S / CORNER.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2007</b>, Loretta Ichord, <i>Double <a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburgers.html>Cheeseburgers</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:quiche.html>Quiche</a>, and Vegetarian <a href = vnd.unilang:burritos.html>Burritos</a></i> (page 48)
<dl><dd>Busy Americans (many women <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> working and not cooking as much) <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> dining on foods such as deep-fried chicken, thick <a href = vnd.unilang:slices.html>slices</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:pizza.html>pizza</a>, double <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburgers.html>cheeseburgers</a></b>, and big slabs of <a href = vnd.unilang:steak.html>steak</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:broodje.html>broodje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plak.html>plak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a></li></ol>

***cheesecake.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cheesecake.html>cheesecake</a> (76735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cheese</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cake</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheesecake.html>cheesecake</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cheesecakes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable and uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">A pie made of sweetened and flavoured cottage cheese or cream cheese, eggs and milk on a <a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>crunchy</a> base.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:cheesecake.html>Cheesecake</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an especially delicious <a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Imagery of one or more scantily clad, sexually attractive young women; <a href = vnd.unilang:pin-ups.html>pin-ups</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> art</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Company policy forbids displaying <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cheesecake.html>cheesecake</a></b> in the locker <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a>.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:chemie.html>chemie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>chemistry, the branch of natural science studying the composition and properties of matter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chemistry, attraction, <a href = vnd.unilang:rapport.html>rapport</a></li></ol>

***cherubijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijn.html>cherubijn</a> (65645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cherubyn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cherubin</i>, reanalyzed as singular, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cherubin</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cherubim</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χερουβίμ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kheroubím</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblical_Hebrew" class="extiw" title="w:Biblical Hebrew">Biblical Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">כְּרוּבִים</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k'ruvím</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> originally plural.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijn.html>cherubijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijnen.html>cherubijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijn.html>cherubijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cherub</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">angel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lamassu-like angel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> six-winged humanoid angel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">putto</span></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cherub</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">affectionate term for a child</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">all angelic senses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">cherub</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***chintz.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chintz.html>chintz</a> (84336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">छींट</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chī̃ṭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chintz.html>chintz</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chintzes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A painted or stained <a href = vnd.unilang:calico.html>calico</a> fabric, originally produced in India, and known for its brightly colored <a href = vnd.unilang:designs.html>designs</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1956</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delano_Ames" class="extiw" title="w:Delano Ames"><a href = vnd.unilang:delano.html>Delano</a> Ames</a>,  chapter 14, in  <cite>Crime out of Mind</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5915292W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He gazed around until on the <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a> of a spinet he spotted a promising collection of bottles, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> a meerschaum pipe and a jar half-full of wasps and apricot jam. He found some glasses which didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> look very clean and polished them on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chintz.html>chintz</a></b> window curtain.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">chintzy</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:chintz.html>chintz</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>  <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***chipper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a> (94616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From English dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nimble; frisky</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of obscure origin. Perhaps akin to Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kjapt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">briskly; impetuously</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kippa</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"to snatch; pull; jerk" gt; Middle English <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kipra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wrinkle; draw tightly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Norwegian <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">kjapp</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fast; brisk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize; catch; <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kip.html>kip</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Exhibiting a lively optimism; in high <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a>, cheerful.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> April 29,  Nathan Rabin,  “TV: Review: THE SIMPSONS (CLASSIC): “Treehouse of Horror III” (season 4, episode 5; originally aired 10/29/1992)”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.avclub.com/articles/treehouse-of-horror-iii,72723/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The idea of a merchant selling both <a href = vnd.unilang:totems.html>totems</a> of pure evil and frozen yogurt (he calls it frogurt!) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> amusing in itself, as <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the idea that frogurt could be cursed, but it’s really the Shopkeeper’s <a href = vnd.unilang:quicksilver.html>quicksilver</a> shift from ominous doomsaying to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></b> salesmanship that sells the sequence.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chippers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fish and chip shop, or more generally a cheap fast food outlet, typically selling <a href = vnd.unilang:chips.html>chips</a> and other deep-fried foods.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A deep frier.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A machine that reduces organic matter to compost; depending on size, whole tree trunks are reduced to sawdust; a woodchipper.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> smoking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An occasional tobacco user, or more generally drug user.</li>
<li>A machine that <a href = vnd.unilang:chips.html>chips</a> potatoes ready to be fried and made into <a href = vnd.unilang:chips.html>chips</a>.</li>
<li>A company that manufactures potato <a href = vnd.unilang:chips.html>chips</a>/potato crisps.
